\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
The {\ttfamily sysio.\+system} smart contract is provided by {\ttfamily block.\+one} as a sample system contract, and it defines the structures and actions needed for blockchain\textquotesingle{}s core functionality.

Just like in the {\ttfamily sysio.\+bios} sample contract implementation, there are a few actions which are not implemented at the contract level ({\ttfamily newaccount}, {\ttfamily updateauth}, {\ttfamily deleteauth}, {\ttfamily linkauth}, {\ttfamily unlinkauth}, {\ttfamily canceldelay}, {\ttfamily onerror}, {\ttfamily setabi}, {\ttfamily setcode}), they are just declared in the contract so they will show in the contract\textquotesingle{}s ABI and users will be able to push those actions to the chain via the account holding the {\ttfamily sysio.\+system} contract, but the implementation is at the EOSIO core level. They are referred to as EOSIO native actions.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Users can stake tokens for CPU and Network bandwidth, and then vote for producers or delegate their vote to a proxy.
\item Producers register in order to be voted for, and can claim per-\/block and per-\/vote rewards.
\item Users can buy and sell RAM at a market-\/determined price.
\item Users can bid on premium names.
\item \doxylink{struct_a}{A} resource exchange system (REX) allows token holders to lend their tokens, and users to rent CPU and Network resources in return for a market-\/determined fee.
\item \doxylink{struct_a}{A} resource market separate from REX\+: {\ttfamily power}. 
\end{DoxyItemize}

\Hypertarget{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_aba0e3afc59fa11936d95f47be61a41df}\index{sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}!bidname@{bidname}}
\index{bidname@{bidname}!sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{bidname()}{bidname()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_aba0e3afc59fa11936d95f47be61a41df} 
void sysiosystem\+::system\+\_\+contract\+::bidname (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{bidder}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{newname}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1asset}{asset}} \&}]{bid}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Bid name action, allows an account {\ttfamily bidder} to place a bid for a name {\ttfamily newname}. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em bidder} & -\/ the account placing the bid, \\
\hline
{\em newname} & -\/ the name the bid is placed for, \\
\hline
{\em bid} & -\/ the amount of system tokens payed for the bid.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyPrecond}{Precondition}
Bids can be placed only on top-\/level suffix, 

Non empty name, 

Names longer than 12 chars are not allowed, 

Names equal with 12 chars can be created without placing a bid, 

Bid has to be bigger than zero, 

Bid\textquotesingle{}s symbol must be system token, 

Bidder account has to be different than current highest bidder, 

Bid must increase current bid by 10\%, 

Auction must still be opened. 
\end{DoxyPrecond}

\Hypertarget{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_a483003285d9c2ad69500c635ac6b5575}\index{sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}!buyram@{buyram}}
\index{buyram@{buyram}!sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{buyram()}{buyram()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_a483003285d9c2ad69500c635ac6b5575} 
void sysiosystem\+::system\+\_\+contract\+::buyram (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{payer}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{receiver}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1asset}{asset}} \&}]{quant}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Buy ram action, increases receiver\textquotesingle{}s ram quota based upon current price and quantity of tokens provided. An inline transfer from receiver to system contract of tokens will be executed.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em payer} & -\/ the ram buyer, \\
\hline
{\em receiver} & -\/ the ram receiver, \\
\hline
{\em quant} & -\/ the quantity of tokens to buy ram with.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
When buying ram the payer irreversibly transfers quant to system contract and only the receiver may reclaim the tokens via the sellram action. The receiver pays for the storage of all database records associated with this action.

RAM is a scarce resource whose supply is defined by global properties max\+\_\+ram\+\_\+size. RAM is priced using the bancor algorithm such that price-\/per-\/byte with a constant reserve ratio of 100\+:1. .5\% fee (round up)

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{delegate__bandwidth_8cpp_source_l00043}{43}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{delegate__bandwidth_8cpp_source}{delegate\+\_\+bandwidth.\+cpp}}.

\Hypertarget{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_a4d11e77e985155ccc97fcdb4eaed04af}\index{sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}!buyrambytes@{buyrambytes}}
\index{buyrambytes@{buyrambytes}!sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{buyrambytes()}{buyrambytes()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_a4d11e77e985155ccc97fcdb4eaed04af} 
void sysiosystem\+::system\+\_\+contract\+::buyrambytes (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{payer}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{receiver}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_a435d1572bf3f880d55459d9805097f62}{uint32\+\_\+t}}}]{bytes}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Buy a specific amount of ram bytes action. Increases receiver\textquotesingle{}s ram in quantity of bytes provided. An inline transfer from receiver to system contract of tokens will be executed.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em payer} & -\/ the ram buyer, \\
\hline
{\em receiver} & -\/ the ram receiver, \\
\hline
{\em bytes} & -\/ the quantity of ram to buy specified in bytes.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This action will buy an exact amount of ram and bill the payer the current market price.

\Hypertarget{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_a9d36ca877a9a15e1c01923f11842a00b}\index{sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}!buyrex@{buyrex}}
\index{buyrex@{buyrex}!sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{buyrex()}{buyrex()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_a9d36ca877a9a15e1c01923f11842a00b} 
void sysiosystem\+::system\+\_\+contract\+::buyrex (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{from}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1asset}{asset}} \&}]{amount}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Buyrex action, buys REX in exchange for tokens taken out of user\textquotesingle{}s REX fund by transferring core tokens from user REX fund and converts them to REX stake. By buying REX, user is lending tokens in order to be rented as CPU or NET resources. Storage change is billed to \textquotesingle{}from\textquotesingle{} account.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em from} & -\/ owner account name, \\
\hline
{\em amount} & -\/ amount of tokens taken out of \textquotesingle{}from\textquotesingle{} REX fund.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyPrecond}{Precondition}
\doxylink{struct_a}{A} voting requirement must be satisfied before action can be executed. 

User must vote for at least 21 producers or delegate vote to proxy before buying REX.
\end{DoxyPrecond}
\begin{DoxyPostcond}{Postcondition}
User votes are updated following this action. 

Tokens used in purchase are added to user\textquotesingle{}s voting power. 

Bought REX cannot be sold before 4 days counting from end of day of purchase. 
\end{DoxyPostcond}


Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{rex_8cpp_source_l00040}{40}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{rex_8cpp_source}{rex.\+cpp}}.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{claimrewards()}{claimrewards()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_ab9da8658bb03830ff0706195fa14fcb0} 
void sysiosystem\+::system\+\_\+contract\+::claimrewards (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{owner}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Claim rewards action, claims block producing and vote rewards. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em owner} & -\/ producer account claiming per-\/block and per-\/vote rewards. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
New metric to be used in pervote pay calculation. Instead of vote weight ratio, we combine vote weight and time duration the vote weight has been held into one metric.

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{producer__pay_8cpp_source_l00076}{76}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{producer__pay_8cpp_source}{producer\+\_\+pay.\+cpp}}.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{closerex()}{closerex()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_ab4f2d94418ed6a1fe42a467b9d72a17b} 
void sysiosystem\+::system\+\_\+contract\+::closerex (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{owner}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Closerex action, deletes owner records from REX tables and frees used RAM. Owner must not have an outstanding REX balance.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em owner} & -\/ user account name.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyPrecond}{Precondition}
If owner has a non-\/zero REX balance, the action fails; otherwise, owner REX balance entry is deleted. 

If owner has no outstanding loans and a zero REX fund balance, REX fund entry is deleted. 
\end{DoxyPrecond}
check for any outstanding loans or rex fund

check for remaining rex balance

\index{deposit@{deposit}!sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{deposit()}{deposit()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_a09c591ec4c299ca55bd73032426128d2} 
void sysiosystem\+::system\+\_\+contract\+::deposit (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{owner}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1asset}{asset}} \&}]{amount}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Deposit to REX fund action. Deposits core tokens to user REX fund. All proceeds and expenses related to REX are added to or taken out of this fund. An inline transfer from \textquotesingle{}owner\textquotesingle{} liquid balance is executed. All REX-\/related costs and proceeds are deducted from and added to \textquotesingle{}owner\textquotesingle{} REX fund, with one exception being buying REX using staked tokens. Storage change is billed to \textquotesingle{}owner\textquotesingle{}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em owner} & -\/ REX fund owner account, \\
\hline
{\em amount} & -\/ amount of tokens to be deposited. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

The \doxylink{struct_init}{Init} action initializes the system contract for a version and a symbol. Only succeeds when\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item version is 0 and
\item symbol is found and
\item system token supply is greater than 0,
\item and system contract wasnt already been initialized.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\Hypertarget{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_acf003e2c76677abb057acedd6db1a2c6}\index{sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}!limitauthchg@{limitauthchg}}
\index{limitauthchg@{limitauthchg}!sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{limitauthchg()}{limitauthchg()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_acf003e2c76677abb057acedd6db1a2c6} 
void sysiosystem\+::system\+\_\+contract\+::limitauthchg (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{account}{, }\item[{const std\+::vector$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} $>$ \&}]{allow\+\_\+perms}{, }\item[{const std\+::vector$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} $>$ \&}]{disallow\+\_\+perms}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

limitauthchg opts into or out of restrictions on updateauth, deleteauth, linkauth, and unlinkauth.

If either allow\+\_\+perms or disallow\+\_\+perms is non-\/empty, then opts into restrictions. If allow\+\_\+perms is non-\/empty, then the authorized\+\_\+by argument of the restricted actions must be in the vector, or the actions will abort. If disallow\+\_\+perms is non-\/empty, then the authorized\+\_\+by argument of the restricted actions must not be in the vector, or the actions will abort.

If both allow\+\_\+perms and disallow\+\_\+perms are empty, then opts out of the restrictions. limitauthchg aborts if both allow\+\_\+perms and disallow\+\_\+perms are non-\/empty.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em account} & -\/ account to change \\
\hline
{\em allow\+\_\+perms} & -\/ permissions which may use the restricted actions \\
\hline
{\em disallow\+\_\+perms} & -\/ permissions which may not use the restricted actions \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\Hypertarget{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_a079655f76d6b6e81339f3f82244fa601}\index{sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}!mvtosavings@{mvtosavings}}
\index{mvtosavings@{mvtosavings}!sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mvtosavings()}{mvtosavings()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_a079655f76d6b6e81339f3f82244fa601} 
void sysiosystem\+::system\+\_\+contract\+::mvtosavings (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{owner}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1asset}{asset}} \&}]{rex}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Mvtosavings action, moves a specified amount of REX into savings bucket. REX savings bucket never matures. In order for it to be sold, it has to be moved explicitly out of that bucket. Then the moved amount will have the regular maturity period of 4 days starting from the end of the day.

{\em rex} & -\/ amount of REX to be moved. \\

\end{DoxyParams}

\Hypertarget{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_a9d200cbff6eb8a4f30fc20b9f11d4dc0}\index{sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}!onblock@{onblock}}
\index{onblock@{onblock}!sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{onblock()}{onblock()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_a9d200cbff6eb8a4f30fc20b9f11d4dc0} 
void sysiosystem\+::system\+\_\+contract\+::onblock (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{ignore$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysiosystem_1_1block__header}{block\+\_\+header}} $>$}]{header}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

On block action. This special action is triggered when a block is applied by the given producer and cannot be generated from any other source. It is used to pay producers and calculate missed blocks of other producers. Producer pay is deposited into the producer\textquotesingle{}s stake balance and can be withdrawn over time. Once a minute, it may update the active producer config from the producer votes. The action also populates the blockinfo table.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em header} & -\/ the block header produced. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
until activation, no new rewards are paid

start the presses

At startup the initial producer may not be one that is registered / elected and therefore there may be no producer object for them.

only update block producers once every minute, block\+\_\+timestamp is in half seconds

Powerup NET and CPU resources by percentage


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em payer} & -\/ the resource buyer \\
\hline
{\em receiver} & -\/ the resource receiver \\
\hline
{\em days} & -\/ number of days of resource availability. Must match market configuration. \\
\hline

\hline

\hline
{\em max\+\_\+payment} & -\/ the maximum amount {\ttfamily payer} is willing to pay. Tokens are withdrawn from {\ttfamily payer}\textquotesingle{}s token balance. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\Hypertarget{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_ac5ae6d98b573572f96b35895e4a5c247}\index{sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}!regproducer@{regproducer}}
\index{regproducer@{regproducer}!sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{regproducer()}{regproducer()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_ac5ae6d98b573572f96b35895e4a5c247} 
void sysiosystem\+::system\+\_\+contract\+::regproducer (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{producer}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classfc_1_1crypto_1_1r1_1_1public__key}{public\+\_\+key}} \&}]{producer\+\_\+key}{, }\item[{const std\+::string \&}]{url}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_a273cf69d639a59973b6019625df33e30}{uint16\+\_\+t}}}]{location}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Register producer action, indicates that a particular account wishes to become a producer, this action will create a {\ttfamily producer\+\_\+config} and a {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsysiosystem_1_1producer__info}{producer\+\_\+info}} object for {\ttfamily producer} scope in producers tables.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em producer} & -\/ account registering to be a producer candidate, \\
\hline
{\em producer\+\_\+key} & -\/ the public key of the block producer, this is the key used by block producer to sign blocks, \\
\hline
{\em url} & -\/ the url of the block producer, normally the url of the block producer presentation website, \\
\hline
{\em location} & -\/ is the country code as defined in the ISO 3166, \href{https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_ISO_3166_country_codes}{\texttt{ https\+://en.\+wikipedia.\+org/wiki/\+List\+\_\+of\+\_\+\+ISO\+\_\+3166\+\_\+country\+\_\+codes}}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyPrecond}{Precondition}
Producer to register is an account 

Authority of producer to register 
\end{DoxyPrecond}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_a40113ff6ec85dc675d64f45089d6e685} 
void sysiosystem\+::system\+\_\+contract\+::regproducer2 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{producer}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_a5d68aec4c925d17b62f0a9b543fabfc5}{sysio\+::block\+\_\+signing\+\_\+authority}} \&}]{producer\+\_\+authority}{, }\item[{const std\+::string \&}]{url}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_a273cf69d639a59973b6019625df33e30}{uint16\+\_\+t}}}]{location}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Register producer action, indicates that a particular account wishes to become a producer, this action will create a {\ttfamily producer\+\_\+config} and a {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsysiosystem_1_1producer__info}{producer\+\_\+info}} object for {\ttfamily producer} scope in producers tables.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em producer} & -\/ account registering to be a producer candidate, \\
\hline
{\em producer\+\_\+authority} & -\/ the weighted threshold multisig block signing authority of the block producer used to sign blocks, \\
\hline
{\em url} & -\/ the url of the block producer, normally the url of the block producer presentation website, \\
\hline
{\em location} & -\/ is the country code as defined in the ISO 3166, \href{https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_ISO_3166_country_codes}{\texttt{ https\+://en.\+wikipedia.\+org/wiki/\+List\+\_\+of\+\_\+\+ISO\+\_\+3166\+\_\+country\+\_\+codes}}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyPrecond}{Precondition}
Producer to register is an account 

Authority of producer to register 
\end{DoxyPrecond}

\Hypertarget{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_a96a701eebb227d312d4a3782ddc0bf3d}\index{sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}!regproxy@{regproxy}}
\index{regproxy@{regproxy}!sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{regproxy()}{regproxy()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_a96a701eebb227d312d4a3782ddc0bf3d} 
void sysiosystem\+::system\+\_\+contract\+::regproxy (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{proxy}{, }\item[{bool}]{isproxy}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Register proxy action, sets {\ttfamily proxy} account as proxy. An account marked as a proxy can vote with the weight of other accounts which have selected it as a proxy. Other accounts must refresh their voteproducer to update the proxy\textquotesingle{}s weight. Storage change is billed to {\ttfamily proxy}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em proxy} & -\/ the account registering as voter proxy (or unregistering), \\
\hline
{\em isproxy} & -\/ if true, proxy is registered; if false, proxy is unregistered.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyPrecond}{Precondition}
Proxy must have something staked (existing row in voters table) 

New state must be different than current state 
\end{DoxyPrecond}

\Hypertarget{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_a522278aee59479ca1bed3c5e5e2f88b3}\index{sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}!rentcpu@{rentcpu}}
\index{rentcpu@{rentcpu}!sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{rentcpu()}{rentcpu()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_a522278aee59479ca1bed3c5e5e2f88b3} 
void sysiosystem\+::system\+\_\+contract\+::rentcpu (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{from}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{receiver}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1asset}{asset}} \&}]{loan\+\_\+payment}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1asset}{asset}} \&}]{loan\+\_\+fund}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Rentcpu action, uses payment to rent as many SYS tokens as possible as determined by market price and stake them for CPU for the benefit of receiver, after 30 days the rented core delegation of CPU will expire. At expiration, if balance is greater than or equal to {\ttfamily loan\+\_\+payment}, {\ttfamily loan\+\_\+payment} is taken out of loan balance and used to renew the loan. Otherwise, the loan is closed and user is refunded any remaining balance. Owner can fund or refund a loan at any time before its expiration. All loan expenses and refunds come out of or are added to owner\textquotesingle{}s REX fund.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em from} & -\/ account creating and paying for CPU loan, \textquotesingle{}from\textquotesingle{} account can add tokens to loan balance using action {\ttfamily fundcpuloan} and withdraw from loan balance using {\ttfamily defcpuloan} \\
\hline
{\em receiver} & -\/ account receiving rented CPU resources, \\
\hline
{\em loan\+\_\+payment} & -\/ tokens paid for the loan, it has to be greater than zero, amount of rented resources is calculated from {\ttfamily loan\+\_\+payment}, \\
\hline
{\em loan\+\_\+fund} & -\/ additional tokens can be zero, and is added to loan balance. Loan balance represents a reserve that is used at expiration for automatic loan renewal. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

void sysiosystem\+::system\+\_\+contract\+::rentnet (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{from}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{receiver}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1asset}{asset}} \&}]{loan\+\_\+payment}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1asset}{asset}} \&}]{loan\+\_\+fund}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Rentnet action, uses payment to rent as many SYS tokens as possible as determined by market price and stake them for NET for the benefit of receiver, after 30 days the rented core delegation of NET will expire. At expiration, if balance is greater than or equal to {\ttfamily loan\+\_\+payment}, {\ttfamily loan\+\_\+payment} is taken out of loan balance and used to renew the loan. Otherwise, the loan is closed and user is refunded any remaining balance. Owner can fund or refund a loan at any time before its expiration. All loan expenses and refunds come out of or are added to owner\textquotesingle{}s REX fund.

\hline
{\em loan\+\_\+fund} & -\/ additional tokens can be zero, and is added to loan balance. Loan balance represents a reserve that is used at expiration for automatic loan renewal. \\
\hline

\Hypertarget{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_ad0bd974e5cf148c501e43661338403e1}\index{sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}!sellram@{sellram}}
\index{sellram@{sellram}!sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{sellram()}{sellram()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_ad0bd974e5cf148c501e43661338403e1} 
void sysiosystem\+::system\+\_\+contract\+::sellram (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{account}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_a414156feea104f8f75b4ed9e3121b2f6}{int64\+\_\+t}}}]{bytes}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sell ram action, reduces quota by bytes and then performs an inline transfer of tokens to receiver based upon the average purchase price of the original quota.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em account} & -\/ the ram seller account, \\
\hline
{\em bytes} & -\/ the amount of ram to sell in bytes.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The system contract now buys and sells RAM allocations at prevailing market prices. This may result in traders buying RAM today in anticipation of potential shortages tomorrow. Overall this will result in the market balancing the supply and demand for RAM over time. the cast to int64\+\_\+t of bytes is safe because we certify bytes is \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}= quota which is limited by prior purchases

.5\% fee (round up)

\Hypertarget{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_a88581cd0c283dcfe488401c2a747612d}\index{sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}!sellrex@{sellrex}}
\index{sellrex@{sellrex}!sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{sellrex()}{sellrex()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_a88581cd0c283dcfe488401c2a747612d} 
void sysiosystem\+::system\+\_\+contract\+::sellrex (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{from}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1asset}{asset}} \&}]{rex}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sellrex action, sells REX in exchange for core tokens by converting REX stake back into core tokens at current exchange rate. If order cannot be processed, it gets queued until there is enough in REX pool to fill order, and will be processed within 30 days at most. If successful, user votes are updated, that is, proceeds are deducted from user\textquotesingle{}s voting power. In case sell order is queued, storage change is billed to \textquotesingle{}from\textquotesingle{} account.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em from} & -\/ owner account of REX, \\
\hline
{\em rex} & -\/ amount of REX to be sold. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
REX order couldn\textquotesingle{}t be filled and is added to queue. If account already has an open order, requested rex is added to existing order.

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{rex_8cpp_source_l00097}{97}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{rex_8cpp_source}{rex.\+cpp}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_a564c7b8087dc53f9e462d1659fbb5ee6} 
void sysiosystem\+::system\+\_\+contract\+::setinflation (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_a414156feea104f8f75b4ed9e3121b2f6}{int64\+\_\+t}}}]{annual\+\_\+rate}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_a414156feea104f8f75b4ed9e3121b2f6}{int64\+\_\+t}}}]{inflation\+\_\+pay\+\_\+factor}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_a414156feea104f8f75b4ed9e3121b2f6}{int64\+\_\+t}}}]{votepay\+\_\+factor}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Change the annual inflation rate of the core token supply and specify how the new issued tokens will be distributed based on the following structure.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em annual\+\_\+rate} & -\/ Annual inflation rate of the core token supply. (eg. For 5\% Annual inflation =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} annual\+\_\+rate=500 For 1.\+5\% Annual inflation =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} annual\+\_\+rate=150 \\
\hline
{\em inflation\+\_\+pay\+\_\+factor} & -\/ Inverse of the fraction of the inflation used to reward block producers. The remaining inflation will be sent to the {\ttfamily sysio.\+saving} account. (eg. For 20\% of inflation going to block producer rewards =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} inflation\+\_\+pay\+\_\+factor = 50000 For 100\% of inflation going to block producer rewards =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} inflation\+\_\+pay\+\_\+factor = 10000). \\
\hline
{\em votepay\+\_\+factor} & -\/ Inverse of the fraction of the block producer rewards to be distributed proportional to blocks produced. The remaining rewards will be distributed proportional to votes received. (eg. For 25\% of block producer rewards going towards block pay =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} votepay\+\_\+factor = 40000 For 75\% of block producer rewards going towards block pay =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} votepay\+\_\+factor = 13333). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\Hypertarget{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_a85a121755169b6464bcb04400c2ec9e1}\index{sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}!setramrate@{setramrate}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setramrate()}{setramrate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_a85a121755169b6464bcb04400c2ec9e1} 
void sysiosystem\+::system\+\_\+contract\+::setramrate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_a273cf69d639a59973b6019625df33e30}{uint16\+\_\+t}}}]{bytes\+\_\+per\+\_\+block}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Set ram rate action, sets the rate of increase of RAM in bytes per block. It is capped by the uint16\+\_\+t to a maximum rate of 3 TB per year. If update\+\_\+ram\+\_\+supply hasn\textquotesingle{}t been called for the most recent block, then new ram will be allocated at the old rate up to the present block before switching the rate.

\Hypertarget{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_a8ad67e13dbed5ec9da9a4d1452dae1aa}\index{sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}!undelegatebw@{undelegatebw}}
\index{undelegatebw@{undelegatebw}!sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{undelegatebw()}{undelegatebw()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_a8ad67e13dbed5ec9da9a4d1452dae1aa} 
void sysiosystem\+::system\+\_\+contract\+::undelegatebw (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{from}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{receiver}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1asset}{asset}} \&}]{unstake\+\_\+net\+\_\+quantity}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1asset}{asset}} \&}]{unstake\+\_\+cpu\+\_\+quantity}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Undelegate bandwidth action, decreases the total tokens delegated by {\ttfamily from} to {\ttfamily receiver} and/or frees the memory associated with the delegation if there is nothing left to delegate. This will cause an immediate reduction in net/cpu bandwidth of the receiver. \doxylink{struct_a}{A} transaction is scheduled to send the tokens back to {\ttfamily from} after the staking period has passed. If existing transaction is scheduled, it will be canceled and a new transaction issued that has the combined undelegated amount. The {\ttfamily from} account loses voting power as a result of this call and all producer tallies are updated.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em from} & -\/ the account to undelegate bandwidth from, that is, the account whose tokens will be unstaked, \\
\hline
{\em receiver} & -\/ the account to undelegate bandwidth to, that is, the account to whose benefit tokens have been staked, \\
\hline
{\em unstake\+\_\+net\+\_\+quantity} & -\/ tokens to be unstaked from NET bandwidth, \\
\hline
{\em unstake\+\_\+cpu\+\_\+quantity} & -\/ tokens to be unstaked from CPU bandwidth,\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyPostcond}{Postcondition}
Unstaked tokens are transferred to {\ttfamily from} liquid balance via a deferred transaction with a delay of 3 days. 

If called during the delay period of a previous {\ttfamily undelegatebw} action, pending action is canceled and timer is reset. 

All producers {\ttfamily from} account has voted for will have their votes updated immediately. 

Bandwidth and storage for the deferred transaction are billed to {\ttfamily from}. 
\end{DoxyPostcond}


Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{delegate__bandwidth_8cpp_source_l00386}{386}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{delegate__bandwidth_8cpp_source}{delegate\+\_\+bandwidth.\+cpp}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_a2812c3906343a7b3685f5c9e30e282c1} 
void sysiosystem\+::system\+\_\+contract\+::unstaketorex (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{owner}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{receiver}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1asset}{asset}} \&}]{from\+\_\+net}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1asset}{asset}} \&}]{from\+\_\+cpu}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Unstaketorex action, uses staked core tokens to buy REX. Storage change is billed to \textquotesingle{}owner\textquotesingle{} account.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em owner} & -\/ owner of staked tokens, \\
\hline
{\em receiver} & -\/ account name that tokens have previously been staked to, \\
\hline
{\em from\+\_\+net} & -\/ amount of tokens to be unstaked from NET bandwidth and used for REX purchase, \\
\hline
{\em from\+\_\+cpu} & -\/ amount of tokens to be unstaked from CPU bandwidth and used for REX purchase.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyPrecond}{Precondition}
\doxylink{struct_a}{A} voting requirement must be satisfied before action can be executed. 

User must vote for at least 21 producers or delegate vote to proxy before buying REX.
\end{DoxyPrecond}
\begin{DoxyPostcond}{Postcondition}
User votes are updated following this action. 

Tokens used in purchase are added to user\textquotesingle{}s voting power. 

Bought REX cannot be sold before 4 days counting from end of day of purchase. 
\end{DoxyPostcond}

\Hypertarget{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_a57f7203c9cb37634e89a66650f5b3b89}\index{sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}!voteproducer@{voteproducer}}
\index{voteproducer@{voteproducer}!sysiosystem::system\_contract@{sysiosystem::system\_contract}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{voteproducer()}{voteproducer()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_a57f7203c9cb37634e89a66650f5b3b89} 
void sysiosystem\+::system\+\_\+contract\+::voteproducer (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{voter}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{proxy}{, }\item[{const std\+::vector$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} $>$ \&}]{producers}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Vote producer action, votes for a set of producers. This action updates the list of {\ttfamily producers} voted for, for {\ttfamily voter} account. If voting for a {\ttfamily proxy}, the producer votes will not change until the proxy updates their own vote. Voter can vote for a proxy {\bfseries{or}} a list of at most 30 producers. Storage change is billed to {\ttfamily voter}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em voter} & -\/ the account to change the voted producers for, \\
\hline
{\em proxy} & -\/ the proxy to change the voted producers for, \\
\hline
{\em producers} & -\/ the list of producers to vote for, a maximum of 30 producers is allowed.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyPrecond}{Precondition}
Producers must be sorted from lowest to highest and must be registered and active 

If proxy is set then no producers can be voted for 

If proxy is set then proxy account must exist and be registered as a proxy 

Every listed producer or proxy must have been previously registered 

Voter must authorize this action 

Voter must have previously staked some EOS for voting 

Voter-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}staked must be up to date
\end{DoxyPrecond}
\begin{DoxyPostcond}{Postcondition}
Every producer previously voted for will have vote reduced by previous vote weight 

Every producer newly voted for will have vote increased by new vote amount 

Prior proxy will proxied\+\_\+vote\+\_\+weight decremented by previous vote weight 

New proxy will proxied\+\_\+vote\+\_\+weight incremented by new vote weight 
\end{DoxyPostcond}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_a752987bb05121075c2c123dd3926630c} 
void sysiosystem\+::system\+\_\+contract\+::voteupdate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{voter\+\_\+name}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Update the vote weight for the producers or proxy {\ttfamily voter\+\_\+name} currently votes for. This will also update the {\ttfamily staked} value for the {\ttfamily voter\+\_\+name} by checking {\ttfamily rexbal} and all delegated NET and CPU.

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyPostcond}{Postcondition}
the voter.\+staked will be updated 

previously voted for producers vote weight will be updated with new weight 

previously voted for proxy vote weight will be updated with new weight 
\end{DoxyPostcond}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysiosystem_1_1system__contract_ae484b84f8281fddd5d9dbcb8b2a4aa85} 
void sysiosystem\+::system\+\_\+contract\+::withdraw (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1name}{name}} \&}]{owner}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsysio_1_1chain_1_1asset}{asset}} \&}]{amount}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Withdraw from REX fund action, withdraws core tokens from user REX fund. An inline token transfer to user balance is executed.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em owner} & -\/ REX fund owner account, \\
\hline
{\em amount} & -\/ amount of tokens to be withdrawn. \\
